There were few people staying on Friday, so I was called directly by the front desk. Therefore, there were few people for breakfast on Saturday, but there were a lot of things, from Suzhou-style dim sum to noodles, bacon, sausage, rice dumplings, fried dough sticks, tofu pudding, oil dumplings, and tea eggs (the most flavorful I have ever eaten). It was not particularly much, but everything was there and the quantity was sufficient. It would not be hurriedly cleaned up because there were only two tables left. Even the pickled cucumbers and dried radishes with white porridge were very deliciousüòã
In fact, I thought it would be an old hotel after reading the reviews before coming here, so I lowered my psychological expectations. The actual decoration is quite new. From the facilities to the service, it can be seen that it is a professional hotel.
The next afternoon, I had nothing to do and went to climb Wangshan. I saw wild monkeys from a distance on the road, and there were small snakes hanging on the trees. It was difficult to walk from Qianyuan Temple down the mountain to Jiulongtan, but it was still an interesting experience.
I ate farmhouse dishes for two nights, and the review list set meal plus extra dishes. The bosses are very good at doing business.
The hot spring is open from 1pm to 10:30pm, and you can experience the small fish pond for free if you stay at the hotel. It's a comfortable and relaxing holiday weekend!

The resort is located in the blessed land of Wangshan, with bamboo forests, lakes and hot springs. It's very comfortable and pleasant, and the air is good^_^ As for the room, I like living in the Shanyu Building the most. It's backed by the bamboo forest, it's quiet, and it's convenient to eat.

Lunch and dinner are on the next floor of the front hall, mainly a la carte and set menus, the chef is very good at cooking ^_^

For fun, besides Tianyi Hot Spring, I was pleasantly surprised to find that the previous golf course has been converted into an equestrian training base, and there are also some small animals, which is pretty good! You can ride a bike, take a walk, or stroll in the bamboo forest with your family and friends in the resort. Going out from the side door, you can also climb Wangshan Mountain and take a look at the observation deck.

The service of the resort is still considerate and meticulous as always.
